{"version":3,"sources":["file:///home/ambooka/Projects/Web/ambooka/src/components/widgets/ExperienceGanttChart.tsx"],"sourcesContent":["'use client'\n\nimport { useState, useEffect } from 'react'\nimport { supabase } from '@/integrations/supabase/client'\nimport { Briefcase } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { format, differenceInMonths, startOfMonth, endOfMonth, addMonths, subMonths } from 'date-fns'\n\ninterface Experience {\n    id: string\n    company: string\n    position: string\n    start_date: string\n    end_date: string | null\n    is_current: boolean\n    description: string | null\n}\n\nexport default function ExperienceGanttChart() {\n    const [experiences, setExperiences] = useState<Experience[]>([])\n    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n    const [viewportStart, setViewportStart] = useState(subMonths(new Date(), 24))\n    const [totalMonths, setTotalMonths] = useState(24)\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        const fetchExperience = async () => {\n            try {\n                const { data, error } = await supabase\n                    .from('experience')\n                    .select('*')\n                    .order('start_date', { ascending: true })\n\n                if (error) throw error\n                setExperiences(data || [])\n\n                if (data && data.length > 0) {\n                    const earliest = startOfMonth(new Date(data[0].start_date))\n                    const today = endOfMonth(new Date())\n                    const diff = differenceInMonths(today, earliest) + 1\n\n                    setViewportStart(earliest)\n                    setTotalMonths(Math.max(diff, 12))\n                }\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error('Error fetching experience:', e)\n            } finally {\n                setLoading(false)\n            }\n        }\n\n        fetchExperience()\n    }, [])\n\n    const months = Array.from({ length: totalMonths }, (_, i) => addMonths(viewportStart, i))\n    const tickInterval = totalMonths > 48 ? 12 : (totalMonths > 24 ? 6 : 3)\n\n    const getPosition = (dateStr: string) => {\n        const date = new Date(dateStr)\n        const diff = differenceInMonths(date, viewportStart)\n        return (diff / totalMonths) * 100\n    }\n\n    const getWidth = (start: string, end: string | null, isCurrent: boolean) => {\n        const startDate = new Date(start)\n        const endDate = isCurrent ? new Date() : (end ? new Date(end) : new Date())\n        const diff = differenceInMonths(endDate, startDate)\n        return (Math.max(diff, 1) / totalMonths) * 100\n    }\n\n    if (loading) return <div className=\"loading-state\">Loading Roadmap...</div>\n\n    return (\n        <div className=\"neo-gantt-widget\">\n            <div className=\"widget-header\">\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n                    <div className=\"header-icon-box\"><Briefcase size={20} /></div>\n                    <h2 className=\"widget-title\">Experience Roadmap</h2>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"gantt-container\">\n                {/* Timeline Header */}\n                <div className=\"timeline-labels\">\n                    {months.filter((_, i) => i % tickInterval === 0).map((month, i) => (\n                        <div key={i} className=\"label-col\">\n                            {format(month, tickInterval >= 12 ? 'yyyy' : 'MMM yy')}\n                        </div>\n                    ))}\n                </div>\n\n                {/* Chart Area with Grid */}\n                <div className=\"chart-area\">\n                    {/* Vertical Grid Lines */}\n                    <div className=\"grid-lines\">\n                        {months.filter((_, i) => i % tickInterval === 0).map((_, i) => (\n                            <div key={i} className=\"grid-line\" />\n                        ))}\n                    </div>\n\n                    {/* Experience Bars */}\n                    <div className=\"rows-container\">\n                        {experiences.map((exp, idx) => {\n                            const left = getPosition(exp.start_date)\n                            const width = getWidth(exp.start_date, exp.end_date, exp.is_current)\n\n                            const isLime = exp.is_current || idx === experiences.length - 1\n                            const isAlt = idx % 2 === 1\n\n                            return (\n                                <div key={exp.id} className=\"gantt-row\">\n                                    <div\n                                        className={`pill-bar ${isLime ? 'lime' : (isAlt ? 'striped' : 'grey')}`}\n                                        style={{\n                                            left: `${Math.max(0, left)}%`,\n                                            width: `${Math.min(100 - Math.max(0, left), width)}%`,\n                                        }}\n                                    >\n                                        <div className=\"pill-content\">\n                                            <span className=\"pill-label\">{exp.position}</span>\n                                            <span className=\"pill-company\">@ {exp.company}</span>\n                                            <div className=\"pill-avatars\">\n                                                <div className=\"mini-avatar\" style={{ background: isLime ? 'black' : 'white' }} />\n                                            </div>\n                                        </div>\n                                    </div>\n                                </div>\n                            )\n                        })}\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <style jsx>{`\n                .neo-gantt-widget {\n                    background: white;\n                    border-radius: var(--neo-radius);\n                    padding: 32px;\n                    box-shadow: var(--neo-shadow);\n                    border: 1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.05);\n                }\n\n                .widget-header {\n                    margin-bottom: 32px;\n                }\n\n                .header-icon-box {\n                    width: 44px;\n                    height: 44px;\n                    background: var(--neo-lime);\n                    border-radius: 12px;\n                    display: flex;\n                    align-items: center;\n                    justify-content: center;\n                    color: black;\n                }\n\n                .widget-title {\n                    font-size: 28px;\n                    font-weight: 800;\n                    color: var(--neo-black);\n                    margin: 0;\n                    letter-spacing: -0.02em;\n                }\n\n                .timeline-labels {\n                    display: flex;\n                    justify-content: space-between;\n                    margin-bottom: 24px;\n                    border-bottom: 2px solid var(--neo-grey);\n                    padding-bottom: 12px;\n                }\n\n                .label-col {\n                    font-size: 11px;\n                    font-weight: 800;\n                    color: var(--neo-dark-grey);\n                    flex: 1;\n                    text-align: center;\n                    text-transform: uppercase;\n                }\n\n                .chart-area {\n                    position: relative;\n                    min-height: 200px;\n                }\n\n                .grid-lines {\n                    position: absolute;\n                    inset: 0;\n                    display: flex;\n                    justify-content: space-between;\n                    pointer-events: none;\n                }\n\n                .grid-line {\n                    border-left: 1px dashed var(--neo-grey);\n                    height: 100%;\n                }\n\n                .rows-container {\n                    display: flex;\n                    flex-direction: column;\n                    gap: 12px;\n                    position: relative;\n                    z-index: 1;\n                }\n\n                .gantt-row {\n                    height: 40px;\n                    position: relative;\n                    width: 100%;\n                }\n\n                .pill-bar {\n rgba(0,0,0,0.05);\n                }\n\n                .pill-bar.lime {\n                    background: var(--neo-lime);\n                    color: black;\n                    z-index: 2;\n                }\n\n                .pill-bar.grey {\n                    background: var(--neo-grey);\n                    color: var(--neo-black);\n                }\n\n                .pill-bar.striped {\n setViewportStart(earliest)\n                    setTotalMonths(Math.max(diff, 12))\n                }\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error('Error fetching experience:', e)\n </div>\n                            )\n                        })}\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <style jsx>{`\n setViewportStart(earliest)\n                    setTotalMonths(Math.max(diff, 12))\n                }\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error('Error fetching experience:', e)\n     const diff = differenceInMonths(date, viewportStart)\n        return (diff / totalMonths) * 100\n    }\n\n    const getWidth = (start: string, end: string | null, isCurrent: boolean) => {\n </div>\n                            )\n                        })}\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <style jsx>{`\n      } finally {\n                setLoading(false)\n            }\n        }\n\n        fetchExperience()\n    }, [])\n\n    const months = Array.from({ length: totalMonths }, (_, i) => 'lime' : (isAlt ? 'striped' : 'grey')}`}\n                                        style={{\n                                            left: `${Math.max(0, left)}%`,\n                                            width: `${Math.min(100 - Math.max(0, left), width)}%`,\n                                        }}\n                                    >\n                                        <div className=\"pill-content\">\n                                            <span className=\"pill-label\">{exp.position}</span>\n                                            <span className=\"pill-company\">@ {exp.company}</span>\n                                            <div className=\"pill-avatars\">\n                                                <div className=\"mini-avatar\" style={{ background: isLime ? </div>\n                            )\n                        })}\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <style jsx>{`\n value, duration = 2000 }: { value: number, duration?: number }) => {\n  const [count, setCount] = useState(0)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let start = 0\n    const end = value\n    if (start === end) return\n\n    let totalMiliseconds = duration\n    let incrementTime = (totalMiliseconds / end)\n\n    let timer = setInterval(() => {\n      start += 1\n      setCount(start)\n      if (start === end) clearInterval(timer)\n    }, incrementTime)\n\n    return () => clearInterval(timer)\n  }, [value, duration])\n\n  return <span>{count}</span>\n}\n\nexport default function About({ isActive = value, duration = 2000 }: { value: number, duration?: number }) => {\n  const [count, setCount] = useState(0)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let start = 0\n    const end = value\n    if (start === end) return\n\n    let totalMiliseconds = duration\n    let incrementTime = (totalMiliseconds / end)\n\n    let timer = setInterval(() => {\n      start += 1\n      setCount(start)\n      if (start === end) clearInterval(timer)\n    }, incrementTime)\n\n    return () => clearInterval(timer)\n  }, [value, duration])\n\n  return <span>{count}</span>\n}\n\nexport default function About({ isActive = false }: AboutProps) {\n  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false)\n  const [selectedTestimonial, setSelectedTestimonial] = useState<Testimonial | null>(null)\n  const scrollTrackRef = setTestimonials(testimonialsResult.data)\n      }\n\n      // Update project count from GitHub (more accurate than DB)\n      try {\n        const githubService = new GitHubService(GITHUB_TOKEN)\n (repos.length > 0) {\n          setProjectCount(repos.length)\n        }\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.error('Error fetching GitHub repos:', e)\n      }\n\n      // Update skills count\n      if (skillsResult.data) {\n        setSkillCount(skillsResult.data.length)\n      }\n\n      // Fetch roadmap info for banner\n      const { data: phasesData } = await (supabase as null\n}\n\nexport default function ExperienceGanttChart() {\n    const [experiences, setExperiences] = useState<Experience[]>([])\n    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n    const [viewportStart, setViewportStart] = useState(subMonths(new Date(), 24))\n    const [totalMonths, setTotalMonths] = useState(24)\n\n    useEffect(() => {\n        const fetchExperience = async () => {\n            try {\n                const { data, error } = await supabase\n                    .from('experience')\n                    .select('*')\n                    .order('start_date', { ascending: true })\n\n                if (error) throw error\n                setExperiences(data || [])\n\n                if (data && data.length > 0) {\n                    const earliest = startOfMonth(new Date(data[0].start_date))\n                    const today = endOfMonth(new Date())\n                    const diff = differenceInMonths(today, earliest) + 1\n\n                    setViewportStart(earliest)\n                    setTotalMonths(Math.max(diff, 12))\n                }\n            } catch (e) {\n                console.error('Error fetching experience:', e)\n            } finally {\n                setLoading(false)\n            }\n        }\n\n        fetchExperience()\n    }, [])\n\n    const months = Array.from({ length: totalMonths }, (_, i) => addMonths(viewportStart, i))\n    const tickInterval = totalMonths > 48 ? 12 : (totalMonths > 24 ? 6 : 3)\n\n    const getPosition = (dateStr: string) => {\n        const date = new Date(dateStr)\n        const diff = differenceInMonths(date, viewportStart)\n        return (diff / totalMonths) * 100\n    }\n\n    const getWidth = (start: string, end: string | null, isCurrent: boolean) => {\n        const startDate = new Date(start)\n        const endDate = isCurrent ? new Date() : (end ? new Date(end) : new Date())\n        const diff = differenceInMonths(endDate, startDate)\n        return (Math.max(diff, 1) / totalMonths) * 100\n    }\n\n    if (loading) return <div className=\"loading-state\">Loading Roadmap...</div>\n\n    return (\n        <div className=\"neo-gantt-widget\">\n            <div className=\"widget-header\">\n                <div className=\"flex items-center gap-3\">\n                    <div className=\"header-icon-box\"><Briefcase size={20} /></div>\n                    <h2 className=\"widget-title\">Experience Roadmap</h2>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <div className=\"gantt-container\">\n                {/* Timeline Header */}\n                <div className=\"timeline-labels\">\n                    {months.filter((_, i) => i % tickInterval === 0).map((month, i) => (\n                        <div key={i} className=\"label-col\">\n                            {format(month, tickInterval >= 12 ? 'yyyy' : 'MMM yy')}\n                        </div>\n                    ))}\n                </div>\n\n                {/* Chart Area with Grid */}\n                <div className=\"chart-area\">\n                    {/* Vertical Grid Lines */}\n                    <div className=\"grid-lines\">\n                        {months.filter((_, i) => i % tickInterval === 0).map((_, i) => (\n                            <div key={i} className=\"grid-line\" />\n                        ))}\n                    </div>\n\n                    {/* Experience Bars */}\n                    <div className=\"rows-container\">\n                        {experiences.map((exp, idx) => {\n                            const left = getPosition(exp.start_date)\n                            const width = getWidth(exp.start_date, exp.end_date, exp.is_current)\n\n                            const isLime = exp.is_current || idx === experiences.length - 1\n                            const isAlt = idx % 2 === 1\n\n                            return (\n                                <div key={exp.id} className=\"gantt-row\">\n                                    <div\n                                        className={`pill-bar ${isLime ? 'lime' : (isAlt ? 'striped' : 'grey')}`}\n                                        style={{\n                                            left: `${Math.max(0, left)}%`,\n                                            width: `${Math.min(100 - Math.max(0, left), width)}%`,\n                                        }}\n                                    >\n                                        <div className=\"pill-content\">\n                                            <span className=\"pill-label\">{exp.position}</span>\n                                            <span className=\"pill-company\">@ {exp.company}</span>\n                                            <div className=\"pill-avatars\">\n                                                <div className=\"mini-avatar\" style={{ background: isLime ? 'black' : 'white' }} />\n                                            </div>\n                                        </div>\n                                    </div>\n                                </div>\n                            )\n                        })}\n                    </div>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n\n            <style jsx>{`\n                .neo-gantt-widget {\n                    background: white;\n                    border-radius: var(--neo-radius);\n                    padding: 32px;\n                    box-shadow: var(--neo-shadow);\n                    border: 1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.05);\n                }\n\n                .widget-header {\n                    margin-bottom: 32px;\n                }\n\n                .header-icon-box {\n                    width: 44px;\n                    height: 44px;\n                    background: var(--neo-lime);\n                    border-radius: 12px;\n                    display: flex;\n                    align-items: center;\n                    justify-content: center;\n                    color: black;\n                }\n\n                .widget-title {\n                    font-size: 28px;\n                    font-weight: 800;\n                    color: var(--neo-black);\n                    margin: 0;\n                    letter-spacing: -0.02em;\n                }\n\n                .timeline-labels {\n                    display: flex;\n                    justify-content: space-between;\n                    margin-bottom: 24px;\n                    border-bottom: 2px solid var(--neo-grey);\n                    padding-bottom: 12px;\n                }\n\n                .label-col {\n                    font-size: 11px;\n                    font-weight: 800;\n                    color: var(--neo-dark-grey);\n                    flex: 1;\n                    text-align: center;\n                    text-transform: uppercase;\n                }\n\n                .chart-area {\n                    position: relative;\n                    min-height: 200px;\n                }\n\n                .grid-lines {\n                    position: absolute;\n                    inset: 0;\n                    display: flex;\n                    justify-content: space-between;\n                    pointer-events: none;\n                }\n\n                .grid-line {\n                    border-left: 1px dashed var(--neo-grey);\n                    height: 100%;\n                }\n\n                .rows-container {\n                    display: flex;\n                    flex-direction: column;\n                    gap: 12px;\n                    position: relative;\n                    z-index: 1;\n                }\n\n                .gantt-row {\n                    height: 40px;\n                    position: relative;\n                    width: 100%;\n                }\n\n                .pill-bar {\n value, duration = 2000 }: { value: number, duration?: number }) => {\n  const [count, setCount] = useState(0)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let start = 0\n    const end = value\n    if (start === end) return\n\n    let totalMiliseconds = duration\n    let incrementTime = (totalMiliseconds / end)\n\n    let timer = setInterval(() => {\n      start += 1\n      setCount(start)\n      if (start === end) clearInterval(timer)\n    }, incrementTime)\n\n    return () => clearInterval(timer)\n  }, [value, duration])\n\n  return <span>{count}</span>\n}\n\nexport default function About({ isActive = false }: AboutProps) {\n  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false)\n  const [selectedTestimonial, setSelectedTestimonial] = useState<Testimonial | null>(null)\n  const scrollTrackRef = Learning in public and documenting my journey from theory to production systems.')\n  // Initialize with fallback to ensure MLOps content is present by default\n  const [expertiseAreas, setExpertiseAreas] = useState<AboutContent[]>(FALLBACK_EXPERTISE)\n  const [testimonials, setTestimonials] = useState<Testimonial[]>([])\n  const [technologies, setTechnologies] = useState<Technology[]>(FALLBACK_TECHNOLOGIES)\n\n  // Dynamic stats for welcome banner (aligned with MLOps roadmap)\n  const [skillCount, setSkillCount] = useState(40)\n  const [projectCount, setProjectCount] = useState(25)\n  const [kpiStats, setKpiStats] = useState<KpiStats>({\n    years_experience: '3+',\n    current_phase: '0/8',\n    expertise_breakdown: { software: 40, cloud_infra: {\n      setLoading(true)\n\n      // Fetch all data in parallel from consolidated schema\n      const [personalInfoResult, skillsResult, testimonialsResult] = await Promise.all([\n        supabase.from('personal_info').select('*').single(),\n        supabase.from('skills').select('*').order('display_order'),\n        supabase.from('testimonials').select('*').order('display_order')\n      ])\n\n      // Set about text from personal_info\n      if (personalInfoResult.data) {\n        const info = personalInfoResult.data\n        if (info.about_text) {\n          setAboutText(info.about_text)\n        }\n\n        // Set expertise from JSONB field\n        if (info.expertise && Array.isArray(info.expertise)) {\n          const expertiseData = info.expertise as unknown as AboutContent[]\n          if (expertiseData.length > 0) {\n            setExpertiseAreas(expertiseData)\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Set KPI stats from JSONB field for the welcome banner\n        if (info.kpi_stats) {\n          setKpiStats(info.kpi_stats as unknown as KpiStats)\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Set technologies from skills table\n      if (skillsResult.data && skillsResult.data.length > 0) {\n        const techData = skillsResult.data.map(skill => ({\n          id: skill.id,\n          name: skill.name,\n          logo_url: skill.icon_url || `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/devicons/devicon/icons/${skill.name.toLowerCase()}/${skill.name.toLowerCase()}-original.svg`,\n          category: skill.category,\n          display_order: skill.display_order || 0\n        }))\n        setTechnologies(techData)\n      }\n\n      // Set testimonials\n      if (testimonialsResult.data && testimonialsResult.data.length > 0) {\n        setTestimonials(testimonialsResult.data)\n      }\n\n      // Update project count from GitHub (more accurate than DB)\n      try {\n        const githubService = new GitHubService(GITHUB_TOKEN)\n        const repos = await githubService.getRepositories(GITHUB_USERNAME, {\n          maxRepos: 100,\n          sortBy: 'updated',\n          includePrivate: Boolean(GITHUB_TOKEN)\n        })\n        if (repos.length > 0) {\n          setProjectCount(repos.length)\n        }\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.error('Error fetching GitHub repos:', e)\n      }\n\n      // Update skills count\n      if (skillsResult.data) {\n        setSkillCount(skillsResult.data.length)\n      }\n\n      // Fetch roadmap info for banner\n      const { data: phasesData } = await (supabase as any).from('roadmap_phases').select('*').order('phase_number')\n      if (phasesData && phasesData.length > 0) {\n        const completedCount = phasesData.filter((p: any) => p.status === years_experience?: string\n  current_phase?: string\n  expertise_breakdown?: {\n    software?: number\n    cloud_infra?: number\n    data?: number\n    ml_ai?: number\n  }\n}\n\nconst StatCounter = ({ value, duration = 2000 }: { value: number, duration?: number }) => {\n  const [count, setCount] = useState(0)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    let start = 0\n    const end = value\n    if (start === end) return\n\n    let totalMiliseconds = duration\n    let incrementTime = (totalMiliseconds / end)\n\n    let timer = setInterval(() => {\n      start += 1\n      setCount(start)\n      if (start === end) clearInterval(timer)\n    }, incrementTime)\n\n    return () => clearInterval(timer)\n  }, [value, duration])\n\n  return <span>{count}</span>\n}\n\nexport default function About({ isActive = false }: AboutProps) {\n  const [isModalOpen, setIsModalOpen] = useState(false)\n  const [selectedTestimonial, setSelectedTestimonial] = useState<Testimonial | null>(null)\n  const scrollTrackRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)\n\n  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)\n  const [aboutText, setAboutText] = useState('Recent Computer Science graduate building toward MLOps Architect. Focused on gaining production experience through hands-on projects in ML deployment, Kubernetes, and cloud infrastructure. Learning in public and documenting my journey from theory to production systems.')\n  // Initialize with fallback to ensure MLOps content is present by default\n  const [expertiseAreas, setExpertiseAreas] = useState<AboutContent[]>(FALLBACK_EXPERTISE)\n  const [testimonials, setTestimonials] = useState<Testimonial[]>([])\n  const [technologies, setTechnologies] = useState<Technology[]>(FALLBACK_TECHNOLOGIES)\n\n  // Dynamic stats for welcome banner (aligned with MLOps roadmap)\n  const [skillCount, setSkillCount] = useState(40)\n  const [projectCount, setProjectCount] = useState(25)\n  const [kpiStats, setKpiStats] = useState<KpiStats>({\n    years_experience: '3+',\n    current_phase: '0/8',\n    expertise_breakdown: { software: 40, cloud_infra: 25, data: 15, ml_ai: 20 }\n  })\n  const [currentFocus, setCurrentFocus] = useState('DevOps')\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchAboutData()\n  }, [])\n\n  const fetchAboutData = async () => {\n    try {\n      setLoading(true)\n\n      // Fetch all data in parallel from consolidated schema\n      const [personalInfoResult, skillsResult, testimonialsResult] = await Promise.all([\n        supabase.from('personal_info').select('*').single(),\n        supabase.from('skills').select('*').order('display_order'),\n        supabase.from('testimonials').select('*').order('display_order')\n      ])\n\n      // Set about text from personal_info\n      if (personalInfoResult.data) {\n        const info = personalInfoResult.data\n        if (info.about_text) {\n          setAboutText(info.about_text)\n        }\n\n        // Set expertise from JSONB field\n        if (info.expertise && Array.isArray(info.expertise)) {\n          const expertiseData = info.expertise as unknown as AboutContent[]\n          if (expertiseData.length > 0) {\n            setExpertiseAreas(expertiseData)\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Set KPI stats from JSONB field for the welcome banner\n        if (info.kpi_stats) {\n          setKpiStats(info.kpi_stats as unknown as KpiStats)\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Set technologies from skills table\n      if (skillsResult.data && skillsResult.data.length > 0) {\n        const techData = skillsResult.data.map(skill => ({\n          id: skill.id,\n          name: skill.name,\n          logo_url: skill.icon_url || `https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/devicons/devicon/icons/${skill.name.toLowerCase()}/${skill.name.toLowerCase()}-original.svg`,\n          category: skill.category,\n          display_order: skill.display_order || 0\n        }))\n        setTechnologies(techData)\n      }\n\n      // Set testimonials\n      if (testimonialsResult.data && testimonialsResult.data.length > 0) {\n        setTestimonials(testimonialsResult.data)\n      }\n\n      // Update project count from GitHub (more accurate than DB)\n      try {\n        const githubService = new GitHubService(GITHUB_TOKEN)\n        const repos = await githubService.getRepositories(GITHUB_USERNAME, {\n          maxRepos: 100,\n          sortBy: 'updated',\n          includePrivate: Boolean(GITHUB_TOKEN)\n        })\n        if (repos.length > 0) {\n          setProjectCount(repos.length)\n        }\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.error('Error fetching GitHub repos:', e)\n      }\n\n      // Update skills count\n      if (skillsResult.data) {\n        setSkillCount(skillsResult.data.length)\n      }\n\n      // Fetch roadmap info for banner\n      const { data: phasesData } = await (supabase as any).from('roadmap_phases').select('*').order('phase_number')\n      if (phasesData && phasesData.length > 0) {\n        const completedCount = phasesData.filter((p: any) => p.status === 'completed').length\n        const totalCount = phasesData.length\n        const currentPhaseObj = phasesData.find((p: any) => p.status === 'in_progress') || phasesData.find((p: any) => p.status === 'upcoming')\n\n        setKpiStats(prev => ({\n          ...prev,\n          current_phase: `${completedCount}/${totalCount}`\n        }))\n\n        if (currentPhaseObj) {\n          setCurrentFocus(currentPhaseObj.target_role || currentPhaseObj.title)\n        }\n      }\n\n    } catch (error) {\n      console.error('Error fetching about data:', error)\n    } finally {\n      setLoading(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Duplicate technologies for seamless infinite scroll\n  const duplicatedTechnologies = [...technologies, ...technologies]\n\n  const openTestimonialModal = Compact Pill */}\n            {area.badge && (\n              <div className=\"inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-[var(--accent-primary)]/5 border border-[var(--accent-primary)]/10 backdrop-blur-sm group-hover:bg-[var(--accent-secondary)]/10 group-hover:border-[var(--accent-secondary)]/20 transition-colors duration-300\">\n                <span className=\"relative flex h-1.5 w-1.5 shrink-0\">\n                  <span className=\"animate-ping absolute inline-flex h-full w-full rounded-full opacity-75 bg-[var(--accent-primary)] group-hover:bg-[var(--accent-secondary)]\"></span>\n                  <span className=\"relative inline-flex rounded-full h-1.5 w-1.5 bg-[var(--accent-primary)] group-hover:bg-[var(--accent-secondary)]\"></span>\n                </span>\n                <span className=\"text-[9px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wider text-[var(--text-tertiary)] group-hover:text-[var(--text-primary)] transition-colors duration-300\">{area.badge}</span>\n              </div>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Typography -
